In the Northern Pavilion Kingdom’s mountains, Huan Yun, Sun Qing, and Bai Bi were the first to awaken, all momentarily bewildered, then straining to consolidate the spiritual energy of their vital gateways while carefully investigating the status of their life items.

However, Sun Qing immediately stored that talisman in her sleeve, seeing her disciple Liu Guibao still in a daze. She then also stowed away that volume of scripture for safekeeping.

Although they had no idea what had transpired, if Sun Qing didn’t dare to take the readily available items before her, what kind of cultivator would she be?

Huan Yun furrowed his brow tightly, “We should have already left that celestial mansion’s ruins.”

The old master was then shocked in his heart, wondering why the items in his talisman-sized object, once filled to the brim with heavenly materials and earthly treasures, now had barely a few left?

Liu Guibao discovered that the bastard named Huai Qian was actually missing.

What a good fellow, he had even deceived her all along. The girl clenched her teeth in anger.

Bai Bi noticed something was amiss, “Where’s Zhan Qing?”

But Liu Guibao’s good-natured temperament was plain to see; she was the first to notice the several packages on the ground and regarded them as opportunities to compete for.

However, Bai Bi also became aware of this, and Gao Ling, the Golden Body Realm warrior, had already regained his senses.

Liu Guibao and her master, Sun Qing, along with Bai Bi, quickly teamed up with Gao Ling, each snatching a heavy package filled with treasures from the celestial mansion.

As they all seized treasures, both sides had their own concerns, so they refrained from interfering with each other.

As for the other package, it was simultaneously eyed by the wild cultivator and the martial arts master standing side by side; in the end, both managed to grasp it, tearing apart the cotton bag, causing numerous treasures to clatter to the ground—over ten in total. The two of them picked up three or four items each, while the rest were commandeered by Huan Yun, Sun Qing, and Bai Bi, showcasing a highly coordinated division of spoils.

If it were a wild cultivator, the first thought would likely be to harm others for treasure, seeking fortune in danger, striving to gain the most advantage.

The remaining survivors who had miraculously avoided death scattered in fear.

In such a cursed place, staying even a moment longer would chill one to the bone.

Huan Yun’s expression shifted slightly; he sensed something amiss and quickly took flight, his sleeves filled with talismans rapidly sweeping out to search the surroundings, also ensuring the safety of Shen Zhenze’s two direct disciples. If that Elder Xu from Longmen discovered the sudden disappearance of the restrictions, he would undoubtedly flee with that talisman-sized item, likely never to return to the Lotus Flower Kingdom or Cloud City before reaching the Golden Core realm.

Fortunately, a dozen miles away, that young couple of cultivators remained safe and sound.

At the same time, one of the talismans, already hundreds of miles away, was shattered.

The old master sneered.

Finally intercepting the Cloud City venerator, the latter, in a fit of rage, shouted, “Huan Yun, are you really going to kill me to the last man?!”

Huan Yun replied, “Return to Cloud City with me and accept your fate under your city lord Shen Zhenze.”

The old venerator raised his hand, gripping that talisman-sized item tightly, “Do you believe I’ll shatter this item directly?”

Huan Yun calmly replied, “The treasures within are not insignificant. If this talisman-sized item shatters, it won’t destroy that immortal metamorphosis and robe either. But I advise you, if you really do that, I will let you die right here, and I will go and apologize to Shen Zhenze alone.”

The old venerator’s expression flickered between anger and uncertainty, “Huan Yun, I will absolutely not go to Cloud City with you. I know Shen Zhenze’s character very well; falling into his hands would be worse than death.”

Huan Yun exclaimed, “If I had known this earlier, I wouldn’t have acted so foolishly! If you hadn’t coveted the treasures in the mountains, bullying two juniors of low cultivation and treating them as puppets, you could have been a hero in Cloud City by now!”

The old venerator replied, “I can hand over the talisman-sized item to you, Huan Yun, but you must take out all the Shrink Earth Talismans as exchange. Lastly, I have one more small request: when you see those two youngsters, tell them that you’ve killed me.”

“Deal!” 

Huan Yun immediately took out a stack of Shrink Earth Talismans without hesitation, slightly spreading them out. Without exception, they were all Shrink Earth talismans. Among them were also two golden talismans.

Huan Yun said solemnly, “A fair trade. Xu, if you dare to play tricks, don’t blame me for being ruthless.”

At the same time, both threw the talismans and the white jade brush tube, and upon the Longmen venerator catching the talisman, he directly activated one of the golden talismans, instantly retreating over a hundred miles away.

Huan Yun sighed, turning back to find those two young individuals, handing over the white jade brush tube, according to his agreement with the Longmen venerator, saying, “Xu has died.”

The young man carefully accepted the white jade brush tube, feeling as if it weighed a thousand pounds, his fingers trembling. Only after storing it in his sleeve did he bow deeply to the old master, tears streaming down his face as he said, “Elder’s great life-saving grace, great protection of the Dao, great treasure-seizing grace; I have no way to repay!”

The young woman was even more distraught, holding her face in her hands, indeed validating the old saying that one who escapes great calamity will surely have future blessings, making her unable to control her emotions.

The harrowing experience of seeking treasures in the mountains would haunt her with nightmares for a lifetime.

Huan Yun smiled and said, “You two are relatively far from others. Take this opportunity to leave quickly. After returning to Cloud City, do not speak of this matter.”

Of course, Huan Yun wanted to roam a bit more and see if there were any missed opportunities.

After the young couple from Cloud City left, Huan Yun felt as if something was amiss, something he hadn’t noticed yet.

The venerator from Cloud City must have forced the secret method of the talisman-sized item from them, which was not surprising. However, Huan Yun was certain that the other party could not have extracted the immortal metamorphosis from the talisman-sized item and hidden it somewhere, nor could he have rolled up that robe to conceal it on himself. Huan Yun had enough discernment for this. Thus, that old venerator’s visit to the mountains had resulted in a net loss; he had only obtained a stack of talismans while losing his position as the chief venerator of Cloud City.

Huan Yun suddenly sighed, chuckling bitterly.

The old master had finally realized one thing.

Understanding why that young man had exhibited a trace of abnormality.

He, Huan Yun, had inexplicably lost the vast majority of heavenly materials and earthly treasures, as well as mountain artifacts within his own talisman-sized item. What then was the scene with the white jade brush tube?

If the immortal metamorphosis and that robe were both gone?

Or if one were left?

What would Shen Zhenze think?

Huan Yun felt somewhat emotional; that young cultivator was truly a good seedling.

What a pity.

He had been killed by that Xu venerator.

Huan Yun, failing to protect the Dao, could only return to Cloud City with that talisman-sized item.

Huan Yun’s gaze turned cold as he pursued.

The old master began to hope that there was still a treasured item left inside.

If not, he would send back the white jade brush tube to Cloud City. If there really was one, then it would be his own opportunity.

Bai Bi, Gao Ling, and the royal venerator from the Lotus Flower Kingdom left together.

All of them felt a heavy mood.

The young lord from Beiting and his family’s venerator had lost everything, with some dead and others surviving.

It was hard to explain.

The Beiting lord’s residence had a tough explanation to make, Zhan Qing’s Nascent Soul master had a tough explanation, and the Water Dragon Sect’s ancestral hall also faced difficulty in explaining.

Bai Bi could only pin her hopes on those treasures to make up for it.

Gao Ling said, “Those two can be killed.”

Bai Bi smiled, “That is indeed so. The opportunities on them will be equally divided between you two.”

Gao Ling, using his martial skills to gather sound into a line, asked the Golden Core disciple from the Water Dragon Sect, “The emperor will ask many questions about this. Afterward, Bai Xianshi’s sect may need to think a lot.”

Bai Bi replied, “Then let’s kill one more.”

Gao Ling said no more.

Bai Bi then said, “Gao Ling, I guarantee you can be the top martial general of the Lotus Flower Kingdom.”

Gao Ling hesitated for a moment before suddenly saying, “I want to change to a chair that a Qi Practitioner cannot sit on but a martial artist can. Once I sit on it, I may not only take the Lotus Flower Kingdom but also the Water Mist Kingdom and Northern Pavilion Kingdom, and Bai Xianshi can take whatever she wants.”

Bai Bi laughed and agreed, “Your ambition is not small, but I believe Gao Ling can sit steadily on that chair.”

The next moment, the venerator from the Lotus Flower Kingdom was killed by Gao Ling with a single punch, his head rolling away, while Bai Bi remained calm, immediately using techniques to destroy the corpse and erase all traces.

There was no need for verbal communication.

Cai Que Prefecture seemed to have become the biggest winner, or at least one of them.

Three came, and three left, all intact, and none could be said to have suffered injury.

They had not acquired a small number of treasures and opportunities.

Wu Qun suddenly spoke, “The black-robed elder who has been on the painting list first twice—will he come looking for trouble with our Cai Que Prefecture?”

The robe on the other party had allowed Wu Qun to recognize his identity.

Sun Qing smiled, “A person who can be friends with Liu Jinglong is not likely to be that despicable.”

Wu Qun still had some worries.

Earlier, Sun Qing had roughly confirmed the quality of that scripture and the talisman; she only said that the latter was a treasured item that only ordinary Fifth Realm cultivators could possess.

After this disaster, apart from Sun Qing and Liu Guibao, Wu Qun no longer trusted any outsiders.

After all, Wu Qun harbored a thought deep in her heart, a thought that frightened her. When Wu Qun asked herself, if she had the means and cultivation of that young sword immortal, could her fellow cultivators, Sun Qing and Liu Guibao, who had enviable cultivation aptitude and Dao fortune, still return to Cai Que Prefecture alive?

Wu Qun did not know the answer.

She did not dare to think further.

Meanwhile, Chen Ping’an, in a secluded mountain, hid the zhao jing at the bottom of a deep pool.

Changing into a new set of clothes, he took off all his robes and donned a simple blue shirt. The young man’s face was now carrying a large bamboo box containing four packages.

Then, as he walked out for over ten miles, he discovered that standing on a high branch beside the mountain path was that familiar old acquaintance, the Golden Body Realm martial artist, Huang Master.

Huang Master smiled, “I knew it was you.”

Chen Ping’an replied, “Why not hide far away?”

Huang Master laughed, “It’s quite funny; even I can’t understand it myself. After leaving that strange place alive, I feel more at ease being near you, Brother Chen.”

Huang Master had completely lost his confidence in how he viewed others' cultivation levels and depth of Dao. The only thing he felt somewhat confident about was judging people’s characters.

Chen Ping’an shook his head, “Don’t provoke me. Let’s each go our own way; we should cherish our fortunes.”

Huang Master shook his conspicuously large backpack, “You’re an expert, Brother Chen. With so many distractions, I’m far behind. After this, Bai Bi and Gao Ling might come looking for me. If they slander me further, with so many items on my back, I might not even be able to leave the Northern Pavilion Kingdom.”

Chen Ping’an asked, “Earlier, I heard you wanted revenge. What for?”

Huang Master’s expression was indifferent as he replied, “In my younger days, I acted impulsively, and I was at fault. However, I never expected that I’d survive, but my entire family of over forty—elders, women, and children—were skinned by cultivators and then dressed in human skins to wear on the dead.”

This purely martial artist spoke calmly, as if simply recounting a story read in a book.

The true suffering in the world is borne by those who endure it; they do not display the heart-wrenching cries seen by others. Even if they do, often after one or two occurrences, they will become even more silent.

Chen Ping’an remained silent.

Huang Master tugged at the corner of his mouth, “Regardless of who you are, I still somewhat trust you. Or rather, I feel lucky and want to take a big gamble. I’m willing to sell you most of the items in my backpack. I only accept immortal money. Once I gather enough, I’ll buy a military armor pill—not the divine person’s armor but a set of Jinwu weaving armor—and then buy the law knife I’ve had my eyes on for a long time. Then I can go do what I should do.”

Chen Ping’an took out a few talismans from his sleeve and tossed them to Huang Master, “These talismans are best for concealing one’s figure and energy. You’re a Golden Body Realm martial artist; you can conceal your traces even better. As long as you hide during the day and move at night, being cautious should be enough for you to leave the Northern Pavilion Kingdom unnoticed.”

Huang Master was momentarily stunned, not immediately reaching for the talismans. Back in the back mountain of the celestial mansion’s ruins, he had used the same method to beat the opponent until they spat blood.

However, at that time, it was more of a test of the other’s depth.

When those talismans drifted far away, Huang Master finally commanded them to his hand, remaining silent for a moment before asking, “What are you really after?”

Chen Ping’an had already continued on his way, leaving behind a sentence: “When calamity strikes, we dare to be angry but can’t speak.”

Just a simple phrase from an outsider.

Yet Huang Master, with a heart of iron and stone and a ruthless demeanor, found his lips trembling, his fists clenched. After loosening one fist and taking a deep breath, he wiped his face.

Suddenly, Huang Master shouted loudly, “Hey, Brother Chen, please stop.”

Chen Ping’an turned around and cursed, “I also have few precious talismans left! I’m just a package master who wakes up early and works hard for a living. I’m not a benevolent child of fortune. Damn it, don’t push your luck. You’re so ungrateful; the old accounts from the mountain haven’t even been settled yet. One punch weighing ten thousand pounds almost broke my old bones… my little bones nearly fell apart…”

Huang Master’s mouth twitched as he nearly wanted to take it back. He suddenly laughed, opening his backpack and shaking it vigorously. In the end, he tossed over three items in succession, “I, Huang Master, can’t be considered a good person, but I don’t wish to owe anyone a favor.”

The “youth” immediately changed his expression, cheerfully receiving the three items and placing them into the bamboo box.

Chen Ping’an rubbed his chin, wondering if they could sit down, share a drink, and slowly discuss business.

Huang Master laughed, “With these talismans, what else would I sell to you? With your business acumen, could I avoid losing money?”

Chen Ping’an laughed, “Too kind, too kind.”

The two parted ways.

Huang Master suddenly asked, “What’s your name? Can you tell me?”

That person did not turn around but raised an arm, lightly clenched his fist, “My name hasn’t changed; Chen Haoren.”

Huang Master couldn’t be bothered to reply.

To hell with your name, Chen Haoren.

But truly, he was a good person.

That person suddenly turned, his sleeves lightly shaking, and in his hand appeared two thick stacks of talismans. He said seriously, “Actually, I still have some offensive talismans here. To be honest, each one is a treasure, and they’re quite affordable…”

Huang Master had already stuck that talisman on himself, not waiting for the man to finish, and raised a middle finger at him, then kicked off the ground, flying away.

Chen Ping’an lamented, “Everyone is so clever; business is hard to do.”

Chen Ping’an walked alone through the lofty mountains, suddenly looking up. A man and a woman were desperately flying away with wind, then they suddenly darted like arrows into a forest, disappearing without a trace.

It was Shen Zhenze’s two direct disciples from Cloud City.

The young man was cautious, leading the girl to alter their route.

The aim was to avoid that potential calamity.

After receiving the talisman-sized item from the old master, they had left with the wind together. But upon immersing themselves in its contents, they discovered not only a few unfamiliar immortal artifacts but also that Elder Xu had treated the talisman-sized item as his own treasure, seeking opportunities that this malicious elder had found for himself. However, the most crucial items—the immortal metamorphosis and that robe—were both missing.

Huan Yun had said that Xu was dead.

Had he forced the secret method of the talisman-sized item from Xu? 

Why did Huan Yun need to go through such lengths? Did he also want to return the white jade brush tube to himself? Was he confident that he wouldn’t dare to leak any secrets to his master?

With such suspicions, one would begin to doubt everything.

And what about the old master Huan Yun? 

In fact, both were clever good people. During this visit to the mountains, even though Huan Yun had had some thoughts, in the end, he did not commit any acts that betrayed his conscience.

Yet ultimately, the trajectory of human hearts spiraled downward, turning from bad to worse.

Huan Yun transformed into a rainbow and pursued, gracefully descending, fixing his gaze upon the two young juniors, his expression indifferent as he asked, “What is the opening incantation of the talisman-sized item?”

The young man pulled the girl behind him and said, “Why does the old master ask when he already knows?”

Huan Yun shouted angrily, “If that were the case, why would I bother to be so redundant?”

The young man smiled bitterly, “How could I guess the intentions of such high beings and immortals?”

Huan Yun then recounted the events.

The young man was slightly startled, saying bitterly, “If that’s the case, why does the old master want to ask about the opening method of the talisman-sized item?”

Huan Yun replied, “So that you both die clearly.”

The young man asked, “We can abandon Cloud City and follow the old master to cultivate.”

Huan Yun looked expressionlessly at the young man behind him, “You must prove yourself.”

The young man suddenly burst into laughter, spitting in disdain, “You’re even worse than those wild cultivators, old master!”

Behind him, the girl felt a chilling sensation as a small concealed blade plunged into the young man’s back. He staggered forward a step, slowly turning his head, confusion written all over his face.

The girl had already retreated ten steps, trembling all over.

Yet she didn’t understand why she was clutching her wrist as if she had been injured.

Huan Yun smiled, “Very good.”

The already gravely injured man turned his head, gazing at the pale-faced girl, his eyes filled with guilt. Tears streamed down his face, but there was no anger, only disappointment and heartbreak as he gently spoke, “Are you foolish? We are all going to die.”

Huan Yun sneered, “Or perhaps you are the clever one.”

Huan Yun turned his head, “Since you are willing to save people, why hide and be sneaky?”

Chen Ping’an stepped out from behind a tree, casting a glance at the girl, whose gaze was filled with regret yet tinged with harshness.

It was just in time; the young man hadn’t died.

Chen Ping’an looked at the old master, “What a sight to behold in broad daylight.” 

(End of Chapter)

 ### Chapter 646: The Swordsman's Dilemma (Part One)

A venerable elder of the Runes Sect, with an ethereal presence.  
Xu Xingjiu from Cloud City was wounded.  
Zhao Qingwan, who had tried and failed to strike a blow.  
And an utterly superfluous young man dressed in a green robe, carrying a large bamboo box on his back.

Huan Yun said, “Why can't the shopkeeper just mind his own business? Why wade into this murky water? Strike while the iron is hot, take the profits, and leave. Earning money safely is the right path.”

Wuqian could identify Huan Yun by his black robe; naturally, he recognized him even more clearly. It wasn't that Chen Pingan was careless; rather, the means of that great demon from Lian Mountain were too unexpected, forcing the White-Clad Goddess and the Green-Clad Deity to unfurl a landscape painting, laying bare everything to those seeking treasures in the mountains.

Still, Huan Yun only speculated on the identity of the young man before him, guessing he was that rogue from Cloud City who sold charms and had the audacity to intervene. Among all the treasure seekers in the mountains, it seemed the only one with the guts and ability to act was that eccentric old man in the black robe.

Once cultivators on the mountain formed their own guesses, whether they were the truth or not became less important.

Chen Pingan chuckled, “Mountain and wild rogues, day in and day out, busy crossing mountains and rivers, sipping clear springs, wading through murky waters—what's so strange about that?”

Xu Xingjiu suddenly spoke, “Huan Zhenren, there's still room for negotiation in this matter.”

Huan Yun shook his head. “The moment I chose to hunt you down, there was no turning back. Xu Xingjiu, you're clever. Smart people shouldn’t say foolish things on purpose.”

Xu Xingjiu understood this well. If Huan Yun truly intended to be aboveboard and had no selfish desires, he wouldn't have chased after him and Zhao Qingwan.

The greater the desire, the narrower the heart, until there’s only a narrow path to tread, forcing one to walk alone.

In fairness, Xu Xingjiu recognized that his earlier choices were also flawed. At the moment Huan Yun handed over the white jade brush tube, he shouldn't have assumed the worst of Huan Yun. Upon learning that the treasures within the square inch had vanished without a trace, he should have chosen to be honest instead of hiding things. If Huan Yun had explained the complexities then, perhaps they wouldn't be in this predicament now. 

However, the ways of the world and the hearts of people were far from simple and clear-cut. The malicious schemes of Xu Gongfu, which ensnared them, made Xu Xingjiu not only feel trepidation but also realize that Huan Yun, as their protector, choosing to stand by and watch was a hidden menace, a concealed intent to kill. Perhaps Xu Gongfu intended to kill them for their treasures, allowing Huan Yun to lay in wait like a yellow sparrow afterward, with his hands completely clean.

Huan Yun did not rush to strike first.  
Chen Pingan also remained composed.  
Many things and people think they have no way back, yet there often is.

Huan Yun was actually in a most awkward position. Xu Xingjiu and Zhao Qingwan from Cloud City undoubtedly needed to be dealt with, but how to negotiate with this rogue who liked to change his identity was fraught with danger, as Huan Yun was uncertain about the other's cultivation level. He couldn’t even determine whether the person was a rune practitioner or the most troublesome sword cultivator on the mountain. Once determined, it would only mean either Huan Yun's death or the other’s demise, in which case all the opportunities and treasures would be his, and Huan Yun would gain profound fortunes.

Chen Pingan suddenly said, “If I'm not mistaken, you Daoists have always spoken about cultivating life without refining one's nature. This is the first ailment of cultivation.”

Huan Yun chuckled lightly. “Easier said than done.”

Chen Pingan replied, “Exactly because it’s so easy to say, it’s hard to do. If done, it becomes a hidden treasure, and virtue is embodied.”

Cultivating both life and nature, achieving great success, is akin to the seamless pagoda revered by Daoists and the fruit of non-leakage honored in Buddhism.

Huan Yun shook his head. “I know you're not very old and definitely not from the Dao sect, so don’t try to match wits with me by quoting those clichés. Why don’t we speak practically, just like we did back at the market in Cloud City?”

Chen Pingan shook his head as well. “As long as you still want to kill two people, we can’t conduct this transaction. Now that we've laid everything bare, aside from your greed and intent to kill, has Xu Xingjiu’s treasure inside that square inch truly compared to the heart you've labored your whole life to cultivate?”

Huan Yun was momentarily speechless, letting out a sigh. “What, you want to persuade me to back off just by talking?”

Xu Xingjiu interjected, “Huan Zhenren, I’m willing to take out all the treasures from that square inch as a price for my life. I sincerely ask you to select one after consideration, to leave behind something to report back to my master. Moreover, I can take an oath using the ancestral hall's secret methods, swearing that I, Xu Xingjiu, will never mention what you have done. In the future, you will still be a guest of honor in Cloud City, and if possible, we can even make you an honorary guardian of our Cloud City.”

Xu Xingjiu had already drawn out the dagger, still a token of their bond, wiped off the blood, and tucked it away, casually bandaging his wounds and swallowing a precious pill he carried from Cloud City.

The wound was not on his back but rather in his heart.  
But Xu Xingjiu was unbothered by it.  

Chen Pingan sighed.  
The smarter Xu Xingjiu acted, the more he assessed the situation and understood the greater picture; in Huan Yun’s eyes, he would only appear as a larger potential threat.  
There was no way around it.  
So, he would change his approach, adopting a style more akin to Beiju Luzhou.  
Otherwise, Huan Yun would resort to killing, risking everything for a big win.

Two flying swords, not yet fully refined into personal artifacts, shot out from two key energy centers, hovering to Chen Pingan's left and right—a slender white rainbow and a deep green glow.

Chen Pingan asked, “Huan Yun, do you want to make another mistake?”

Huan Yun’s sleeves billowed as countless talismans floated out, forming a protective formation around him, tremblingly saying, “Is it you, together with Liu Jinglong, who offered swords at the Festival of Lotus in the Fuhua Kingdom?!”

Chen Pingan inquired, “What do you think?”

Huan Yun sighed deeply. “No wonder, no wonder.”

Chen Pingan turned to Xu Xingjiu. “What do you say?”

Xu Xingjiu replied, “Senior, I will take my junior sister back to Cloud City.”

Zhao Qingwan cried out, “I won’t go! Xu Xingjiu, just kill me!”

Xu Xingjiu smiled bitterly. “Let’s not do anything foolish. There’s no hurdle we can’t overcome. Qingwan, if you trust me, just leave this place with me. We were the way we were before, and we can be the same in the future. I have no grudges here; you just need to clear your own heart, and nothing will have changed—perhaps it can even be better. Qingwan, everyone makes mistakes; don’t be afraid, we can correct our wrongs.”

Zhao Qingwan, like a person possessed, turned pale, but her eyes were red. “We can’t go back, it’s already too late. You either kill me or I kill you; otherwise, let’s die together. In our next life, we can be a couple, ensuring we’ll love each other forever. Xu Xingjiu, how about that?”

Xu Xingjiu’s expression turned serious, drawing the dagger and gently tossing it to Zhao Qingwan. He looked around, surrounded by dense forest, and self-mockingly said, “Husband and wife are like birds of the same forest; when disaster strikes, they fly separate ways. Yet, we haven’t even become partners yet, and it’s already come to this. Qingwan, give me another stab. Otherwise, even if I have to tie you up, I’ll take you back to Cloud City. I promised to become your partner in this lifetime; I, Xu Xingjiu, will keep my word.”

Zhao Qingwan held the dagger, staring blankly at Xu Xingjiu. Suddenly, she smiled, tears in her eyes, her lips moved silently, seemingly saying three words.

Xu Xingjiu’s eyes brimmed with tears.  
It had always been this way; he adored her expressive eyes.

Years ago, when the master brought a little girl to Cloud City, the boy looked at her as she tilted her head, her round eyes wide open.  
The boy made a face.  
The little girl was so frightened that she began to cry.

Year after year, Cloud Sea high above held people’s homes.  
Zhao Qingwan suddenly thrust the dagger towards her heart.  

In the next moment, Xu Xingjiu was in front of her, gripping the dagger with his hand, blood spurting.  
Xu Xingjiu softly said, “Qingwan, we’ve both died once; can we start anew in this lifetime?”

Zhao Qingwan let go of her grip, squatting down, cradling her face in her hands.  
Xu Xingjiu dropped the dagger, crouched down, and gently embraced her. Just as he was about to pat her back soothingly, he remembered his palm was covered in blood; he gently turned his hand over and stroked with the back of his hand, whispering, “Don’t be afraid, don’t be afraid. You always resented me for not saying I liked you, right? In the future, don’t ask again. What man often speaks of his true feelings?”

Huan Yun's expression was complex.  
Chen Pingan asked, “Huan Yun, you seem to have left a child back in Cloud City?”

Huan Yun flew into a rage. “Never harm the family!”

Chen Pingan said, “I intend to learn from you; I will sever the roots of this trouble.”

Huan Yun questioned, “Are you forcing me to perish with you?”

Chen Pingan replied, “Do you think you’re worth it?”

Huan Yun appeared as if he aged a hundred years in an instant, his weariness evident. “Enough. A lifetime of reputation ruined in an instant. From now on, I will never set foot in Cloud City again. Regardless of how Xu Xingjiu and Shen Zhenze target me, it is all a result of my own actions.”

Chen Pingan shook his head. “Whether you see me as a good person or a bad one is irrelevant, but I advise you not to treat me as a fool.”

Huan Yun gritted his teeth. “What do you want?! You really want to kill me, Huan Yun, and then kill my grandson? I refuse to believe you can do it…”

Chen Pingan interrupted Huan Yun’s words and slowly said, “I’ll accompany you on this soul-searching journey.”

Huan Yun was taken aback.  
Chen Pingan added, “Do you have a talisman boat? We should best travel back to Cloud City together.”

In the end, two valuable talisman boats, as large as mundane ferries, slowly ascended, heading towards Cloud City.  
One carried four people; the other bore a massive treasure pulled from a deep pool, both boats protected by Huan Yun’s illusionary talismans.

On one end of the boat sat Xu Xingjiu and Zhao Qingwan side by side.  
Chen Pingan and Huan Yun sat back to back against the ship's wall.

Chen Pingan sat cross-legged, leaning against the large bamboo box, and turned to speak to the girl: “Cherish this hard-earned good fortune. In the future, as you both interact, you must not take this incident lightly, nor should you deliberately avoid today’s turmoil. Otherwise, it will lead to trouble sooner or later, and it would be sadder to die late than to die early. If both of you can pass this heart hurdle, you and Xu Xingjiu will truly become celestial partners. The path of cultivation is fraught with trials; self-examination is the hardest. This may be the tribulation you both need to refine your hearts; whether you can turn misfortune into fortune depends on whether you are willing to consider the gains and losses therein.”

Then Chen Pingan turned to Xu Xingjiu and said, “Even if you truly don’t mind this, on her side, a mistake is still a mistake, and a grave mistake is a grave mistake. So don’t comfort her with empty words. You, Xu Xingjiu, must clarify this for yourself; otherwise, it will only make her feel more guilty and self-conscious, feeling unworthy of you. In the end, you may either turn against each other or become strangers. Ultimately, it’s still your fault for not being good enough. There’s no way around it; since you, Xu Xingjiu, have chosen to be the good person, you must pay the price for it.”

Xu Xingjiu held Zhao Qingwan's hand and nodded with a smile.  
In the realm of their hearts, it felt like they had found light among the shadows, the rain clearing to reveal a bright sky, and they sensed they were on the brink of breaking through a bottleneck.

After hearing Chen Pingan’s words, Zhao Qingwan seemed to unlock some of the knots in her heart, slightly loosening the still unresolved ones.  
Though they seemed to be holding hands, she had always been the one held by Xu Xingjiu. Now, she finally grasped Xu Xingjiu’s hand, tightening her grip slightly.

Huan Yun remained silent, eyes closed in contemplation.  
Since Chen Pingan had made clear his identity as the “Sword Immortal” who had ascended with Qi Jinglong, he no longer hid it, removing the facade of youth and restoring his true appearance, donning the black robe of the hundred-eyed Tuo Tuo, now brimming with spiritual energy, which Chen Pingan could use for refining.

As for whether Huan Yun would think there was an opportunity to exploit, that would depend on this elder’s luck.  
In this world, when villains harbor malicious thoughts and act wickedly, once they suffer losses, should they still blame others for not marking them as “experts?”

Then Xu Xingjiu formulated a strategy that would neither betray his master Shen Zhenze nor harm Cloud City’s interests, while also preserving Huan Yun’s reputation.  
Even Xu Xingjiu’s injuries had a reasonable yet unexpected explanation.  
Seamless. Logical.

Chen Pingan had no objections.  
Though Huan Yun still kept his eyes shut, he nodded gently.  
The two talisman boats directly entered Cloud City, where Shen Zhenze personally awaited them.

Xu Xingjiu recounted the “sequence of events”—the malicious plot of Xu Gongfu and the timely protection offered by the elder Huan Yun.  
Then, they encountered this fellow practitioner, the senior who had sold charms at their market, and together they overcame difficulties in the heavily fortified ruins of the immortal palace.

Shen Zhenze was taken aback, surprised by the myriad dangers faced.  
As for how they managed to escape, not only Xu Xingjiu but even Huan Yun remained in the dark. Thus, Shen Zhenze increasingly felt that his two disciples had indeed been immensely blessed on this trip down the mountain, as they returned safely, not only alive but also bringing back several treasures from the white jade brush tube, which was no small feat. Without a second thought, Shen Zhenze divided the four treasures from the square inch among the four: Huan Yun, the elder Chen, Xu Xingjiu, and Zhao Qingwan, each receiving one.

Huan Yun could not refuse and had to choose first, selecting the least valuable and lowest-ranked item.  
Chen Pingan, unabashed, directly picked the most appealing one: a pair of couplets with golden bats on a blue background.

“The wind and rain beyond the mountain, three-foot sword;  
When there’s business, draw the sword and descend the mountain.  
In the clouds, flowers, and birds, a room full of books;  
Without worries, reading brings forth sages.”

Xu Xingjiu let Zhao Qingwan choose first. Zhao Qingwan’s gaze was filled with resentment, but Xu Xingjiu recalled the teachings of that sword immortal and no longer hesitated, selecting one himself.

Due to the serious nature of the situation, involving the defection of a chief offering from Cloud City, the celebration feast attended by only five people quickly dispersed.  
Shen Zhenze, of course, wanted to discuss this matter with Xu Xingjiu repeatedly. It wasn’t that he didn’t trust his most valued disciple, but he worried there were critical aspects Xu Xingjiu hadn’t considered, so as a master, he had to help remedy one or two things.

To be honest, many times Shen Zhenze felt that he, the city lord of the Golden Core, was unworthy of having Xu Xingjiu as his disciple.  
However, such grand truths could not be spoken aloud and could only be kept in his heart.

In the secret chamber of Shen Zhenze’s place of cultivation, Zhao Qingwan sat quietly beside her senior brother Xu Xingjiu as usual, watching him converse with their master.  
Yet, thinking of how her most respected master, Xu Xingjiu, had so earnestly deceived him today—though there was not an ounce of malice behind it—was a refreshing event she had never dared to imagine before. Zhao Qingwan couldn’t help but smile, bowing her head to hide her slight amusement, but as she laughed, tears quietly rolled down her cheeks.

Shen Zhenze noticed her unusual behavior and gently asked, “Qingwan, what’s wrong?”

Zhao Qingwan became flustered, at a loss for words.  
Xu Xingjiu chuckled, “Master, before we descended the mountain, Qingwan kept saying she was a burden. But back then, she said it jokingly to me. Looking back, oh? It turns out it really is so. So on the way here, I’ve been crying and laughing, so please don’t mind her. I’ll scold her a bit later for not cultivating her heart enough, but after the scolding…”

Xu Xingjiu laughed too.  
Shen Zhenze asked in confusion, “What is it?”

Xu Xingjiu stood up, performed a respectful bow, and solemnly said, “I humbly request my master to agree to my union with Qingwan as partners.”

Shen Zhenze laughed heartily, “Does it matter if I don’t agree? You two don’t even agree!”

Zhao Qingwan lifted her head, emotions mixed, and fell to the ground, weeping loudly.  
Shen Zhenze looked at Xu Xingjiu, his expression serious.  
Xu Xingjiu shook his head, his gaze clear.  
Shen Zhenze chose not to press further.

Any Golden Core cultivator in the world, regardless of their actual realm, may have high or low cultivation but possess a mind that ordinary people cannot match.  
While it’s rare for a Golden Core to slay a Nascent Soul, it’s not uncommon for them to scheme against one.  
Not just Golden Cores, but all cultivators face this.

On the path of cultivation, how can one be careless?  
Chen Pingan temporarily resided in a mansion in Cloud City.  
It was the private residence of the old cultivator Xu Gongfu, a figure second only to Shen Zhenze in Cloud City, who had neither family nor disciples.  
Thus, Chen Pingan settled down quietly.

At this moment, with Huan Yun, they once again faced each other in a viewing pavilion atop a faux mountain.  
Huan Yun asked, “When will this journey of introspection come to an end?”

Chen Pingan bent down and took out an item from the bamboo box—something Master Huang had refused to owe anyone a favor, a jade charm with cloud patterns, green and measuring an inch wide and two inches long, suitable for hanging against the heart. It seemed to be made of the same material as the tiles on the mountaintop Daoist temple, with just a slight difference in texture, something Chen Pingan couldn’t quite pinpoint.

On one side was an ancient inscription: “Heart.”  
On the other was a couplet:  
“In the fields, the ditches are dim and foggy;  
The doors and gates wash away the essence of the sun and moon.”

“It’s a heart charm for the Dao sect, though it’s quite rare these days.”  
Huan Yun merely glanced at it and commented nonchalantly, “In our Daoism, there has long been the saying that the Dao collects the void, which is the heart’s cultivation. In fact, Confucianism, Buddhism, and Daoism all share broadly similar teachings.”

Chen Pingan held it in his palm, slowly tracing it, smiling, “You understand the principles, and you likely understand them better than I do.”

Huan Yun chuckled, “Unfortunately, I’m not as accomplished as the Sword Immortal.”

Chen Pingan asked, “Is it because one has high cultivation that one understands principles, or is it because principles are understood that one achieves high cultivation?”

Huan Yun replied, “The realm of a cultivator is often unrelated to principles.”

Chen Pingan nodded, “Some principles are indeed like that.”

Huan Yun said, “I still have to thank you for not heading straight to my residence.”  
Chen Pingan gently placed the heart charm on the table, taking out the other two gifts from Master Huang—a jade bracelet inscribed with a palindromic poem, within which fireflies flickered. A quaint tree gnarled pot, slowly absorbing spiritual energy.  

These were all fine items.  
Only Chen Pingan couldn’t discern just how valuable they were.  
The reason why Master Huang’s large bag seemed so bulky was due to one significant item inside. When Master Huang jostled the bag to retrieve items, the delicate clinks hinted at him having acquired something remarkable. Besides the largest item, there were at least seven or eight other assorted treasures, but he ultimately offered Chen Pingan these three. Despite this, Master Huang’s collection was still rich, but Chen Pingan felt that no matter how good the items were, they wouldn't surpass the Daoist book of Liu Guibao and the token of the mansion lord, Sun Qing.

The reason Chen Pingan knew this was purely due to his own nature.  
It seemed inconsequential not to know. After all, he wouldn’t be competing with Master Huang.  
Whether one knows or not, does it really make a difference?  
Of course, it does—and it’s a world apart.

The veins of the human heart flow like water through a riverbed; trivial matters are like water, while the myriad changes of the world are as numerous as the hairs on cattle. The heart is that riverbed. If you can navigate it and gather it, then it becomes a great river, deep and quiet in demeanor.  
Ultimately, one can be like that dragon, entering the sea.

Chen Pingan was on a path along the water for the young green-clad child.  
But in reality, all along, Chen Pingan's own cultivation of heart was like a dragon raising its head from the well, quietly traversing the river.

Is it hard to kill Huan Yun or Zhao Qingwan with a few strikes?  
Is it really that difficult?  
What’s hard about it?  
He has always done simple things.  
Perhaps this isn’t considered cultivation.

Huan Yun continued, “The jade bracelet itself is made from good material, and there are talisman masters who use poetry as a form of talismanic formation. Over time, it creates a scene like fire in water. This tree gnarled pot can help practitioners of Qi gather spiritual energy from heaven and earth while also refining it into suitable wood element spiritual energy. It’s not a treasure, but in the hands of those who earnestly cultivate wood techniques, it’s a valuable item they wouldn’t trade for anything.”

With this explanation, it spared Chen Pingan a lot of trouble. He wouldn’t sell this gnarled pot, and as for the jade bracelet, even if he were to sell it, he would demand an exorbitant price.  
Nevertheless, Chen Pingan still asked, “What do you think this bracelet could sell for in snowflake coins?”

Huan Yun replied, “Why not several grain rain coins?”  
Chen Pingan shook his head. “Old Zhenren, you really don’t know how to count money wisely.”

Huan Yun then stated a price—two grain rain coins.  
Even for Golden Core cultivators like Sun Qing from the Caique Mansion or Bai Bi from the Water Dragon Sect, one grain rain coin was no small sum.  
Many practitioners below the Golden Core, especially those in the Fifth Realm, might not even be able to gather a single grain rain coin as their savings, aside from their personal treasures. Even wealthy mountain and wild cultivators seldom carried several grain rain coins on them, usually saving only small summer coins for emergencies. If they truly needed money, converting small summer coins into snowflake coins was easy; any immortal ferry in the world would do just fine.

Chen Pingan smiled, “Old Zhenren, you have good taste.”  
Huan Yun’s expression was desolate. “Good taste doesn’t matter. I’m still no match for the Sword Immortal’s flair.”

Chen Pingan said, “Old Zhenren, you really need to change your temperament of being unable to stand others doing well.”  
Huan Yun sneered, “How could a mere Golden Core like me dare not listen to a Sword Immortal’s principles?”

Chen Pingan shot him a glance and said, “I’m just afraid that some principles you finally manage to listen to, you won’t be able to accept.”  
Huan Yun fell silent.

Chen Pingan, however, smiled, “But I’m a bit better than you, as I love to hear people calmly explain principles. Old Zhenren, why don’t we chat about the knowledge of talismans? Let’s spar a bit and benefit each other.”  
Huan Yun looked at this man, truly a character difficult to predict; he felt restless and unhappy, prompting the old Zhenren to involuntarily sarcastically suggest, “How about I just take out a few talisman secrets? Lay them on the table, and when Chen Sword Immortal says to turn the page, I’ll turn it?”

Chen Pingan ignored him, carefully putting away the jade bracelet and gnarled pot into the bamboo box, then cheerfully opened a package from the box and placed an item heavily on the table.  
It was a piece of blue brick pried from the ground of the mountaintop Daoist temple.

Huan Yun began to close his eyes and meditate.  
This blue brick might very well be considered a treasured item by ordinary immortal families, meant to safeguard their homes.  
After a moment of thought, Chen Pingan took out writing materials and began to meticulously sketch the architectural style of the immortal palace ruins, especially the white jade arch bridge.  
Only the mountaintop Daoist temple would not be carelessly drawn on paper.

After finishing two sheets of paper, Chen Pingan said, “Old Zhenren, can you help me out? Draw the large buildings on the back mountain?”

Huan Yun swallowed his anger and took out pen and paper from the square inch, beginning to draw.  
Chen Pingan stood up, walked around the stone table, and looked at the old Zhenren drawing, remarking, “You have to draw better than I do, no wonder you’re a talisman master.”  
Huan Yun was about to stop.  
That person was raising his hand.  
Huan Yun had no choice but to continue.

There was no other way; though the words from that person were flattering, he held a piece of blue brick in his hand.

The next day, the item placed in the courtyard of the private residence, the immortal palace's algae well, was something Shen Zhenze of Cloud City absolutely wanted to buy.  
This Golden Core city lord seemed determined, sincerely stating that even if he had to sell everything he owned, he wanted to buy this invaluable item that could stabilize the fortunes of the mountains and waters, even offering to trade all the properties and shops in a certain street of Cloud City.

Chen Pingan did not immediately agree.  
Huan Yun also had thoughts regarding this priceless algae well.  
He just didn’t dare to voice them.  
Shen Zhenze was still hoping Huan Yun would help plead, but just thinking about that blue brick in the guy’s hand made Huan Yun’s head ache, so he declined Shen Zhenze’s offer.

At that moment, Shen Zhenze laughed in anger. “Good, you old Zhenren, don’t tell me you want to compete with me for this item?”  
Huan Yun felt no shame and straightforwardly replied, “Fortune is hard-earned; each relies on their own abilities.”  
Shen Zhenze, left with no choice, could only say that since the item had already landed in the courtyard of Cloud City, it should stay there and take root.  
Huan Yun laughed, “Walk slowly, no need to see me off.”  
Shen Zhenze departed in a huff.

*(End of Chapter)*

 ### Chapter 647: The Swordsman's Business (2)

Chen Ping'an made another trip to the market outside Cloudy Peak City, setting up shop as a talisman vendor this time, only selling talismans and nothing else. 

Squatting by the roadside with his hands tucked in his sleeves, he didn’t shout out to attract customers; he simply answered any inquiries that came his way. 

He recalled the news he had seen in the Mountain and Water Gazette about the wild cultivator Huang Xi set to fight the martial artist Xiu Niang at Refining Stone Mountain in a couple of days. Chen Ping'an certainly wouldn’t miss it.

After Huan Yun departed yesterday, Chen Ping'an began to carefully calculate the gains from his treasure-seeking journey. 

Aside from the scraps of wood from the deities’ statues at the Taoist temples, he had thirty-six blue bricks from the temples, a total of one hundred twenty-two pieces of emerald-green glazed tiles, droplets of water from the green bamboo leaves inside his Sword Nourishing Gourd, and, of course, a vast number of bamboo leaves and branches. 

For the time being, he was also nurturing a cluster of fragmented sword qi stored within the Gourd. Additionally, he had yet to read the last book he obtained, along with the four items gifted by Huang— a bronze mirror, a fasting token, a jade bracelet, and a tree galls pot. 

He had to factor in the rich spiritual energy absorbed into his robe from the pavilion he had visited, along with the extra trip down the River of Time.

The old immortal Huan Yun had entrusted a young child to Shen Zhenze early this morning, asking a guest elder to quietly take the child back to his mountain. 

Chen Ping'an would not interfere. Without peace of mind, how could one cultivate tranquility?

During the midnight hour, when all was still— a state highly regarded in Daoism— it was akin to the Buddhist practice of lighting incense, which could happen at any time.

Suddenly, Chen Ping'an looked up with a smile and greeted someone. 

Xu Xingjiu squatted across from his stall, but found herself at a loss for words.

Chen Ping'an asked, "Are you well?"

Xu Xingjiu’s smile blossomed, "I’m well."

Chen Ping'an nodded, "That’s good to hear."

Xu Xingjiu asked, "Can I buy some talismans from you, senior?"

Chen Ping'an replied, "Of course, guests are welcome. However, the price of each talisman is fixed; you don’t need to bring out that treasure you previously acquired, as I won’t accept it here."

Xu Xingjiu’s expression turned awkward. 

She indeed carried a treasure with her—two, in fact—yet not a single piece of celestial money. She felt she had miscalculated. 

After their heart-to-heart last night, she and Zhao Qingwan agreed to present their treasures as a token of gratitude.

Chen Ping'an laughed, "Since you won’t be able to partake in your joyous occasion, don’t feel guilty. Just think of that treasure as my red envelope for you."

Xu Xingjiu said, "Then I won’t delay you in your business any longer."

Chen Ping'an waved his hand, "If you truly want to thank me, bring some wealthy souls over."

Xu Xingjiu forced a smile, "I’ll try my best."

Chen Ping'an chuckled, "Do you seriously believe I’m joking? If it’s a matter of conscience, then it’s best not to pursue it."

Xu Xingjiu was left speechless. 

Chen Ping'an rubbed his forehead, "I was just saying it casually. Why do you take everything to heart? Isn’t it exhausting?"

Xu Xingjiu replied, "From observing your words and actions, senior, everything aligns with the Dao."

Chen Ping'an nearly broke into a cold sweat, "My mountain gate isn’t accepting disciples at the moment."

Xu Xingjiu was baffled, yet she still bowed respectfully and took her leave.

What a remarkable swordsman elder, whose words were full of profound meanings.

In the distance, a graceful young woman stood, hesitant to approach the talisman stall.

Chen Ping'an looked up and smiled, nodding in acknowledgment.

Zhao Qingwan gave a respectful bow.

Xu Xingjiu held her hand, and Zhao Qingwan bowed her head.

Xu Xingjiu observed her, speaking softly. 

Chen Ping'an kept his hands tucked in his sleeves, watching this somewhat familiar scene unfold. He felt that even though human hearts may waver, there would still be reunions amidst the mountains and waters—how delightful it was!

However, business at his stall had been far from booming, leaving something to be desired.

By the end of the day, he had sold only a few talismans, earning thirty snowflake coins.

Upon arriving at the residence left behind by the former priest, Chen Ping'an squatted in the yard, carefully polishing the slanted well against the wall, occasionally breathing out mist towards it, nearly pressing his forehead against the well.

Huan Yun, watching from the side, had a strange expression.

Could this truly be a swordsman capable of journeying the mountains with Liu Jinglong?

Finally, Huan Yun spoke, "Why did you ask me to send a message to the Patriarch Hall of the Colorful Sparrow House? You want Sun Qingwu to come see this?"

Chen Ping'an turned his back to the old immortal and said, "If you see Xu Xingjiu and Zhao Qingwan as unexpected, then Sun Qing and her three companions are also unexpected— and they could easily draw calamity. Since you think this way, I want to see if I can turn this unexpected event into something good while making a fortune. Regardless of whether the well ends up being sold to the Colorful Sparrow House, Sun Qing and the others should remember the incense connection you have with Huan Yun. Besides, you mentioned that Sun Qing, especially her disciple Liu Guibao, are both smart and straightforward people, making them worth a try."

Huan Yun asked, "Why help me so?"

Chen Ping'an gently wiped the exquisite patterns on the well with his sleeve, never turning around, and slowly said, "I’m helping the old gentleman who opened the door for me."

Huan Yun sighed, "The heart’s burdens are hard to bear."

Chen Ping'an smiled, "In the marketplaces below the mountain, every year is tough as the last."

Huan Yun fell silent.

Chen Ping'an continued, "As for Bai Bi of the Water Dragon Sect, I can’t help there. As a mere wild cultivator and talisman vendor, I feel a little intimidated in their presence."

Huan Yun said, "They are currently also in a quandary. I can find an opportunity to meet Bai Bi quietly and resolve this hidden danger."

After all, the incident involving Xu Xingjiu and Zhao Qingwan was a matter that Colorful Sparrow House’s Sun Qing and Water Dragon Sect’s Bai Bi seemed to know nothing about, yet they were fully aware of everything.

What they didn’t know was what lay ahead.

It was fortunate that these two Golden Core cultivators remained oblivious.

Only the young swordsman before them was aware.

Chen Ping'an said, "I believe it would be better for the high-level cultivators of the Water Dragon Sect to come find you, Huan Yun; this kind of favor is what people like Bai Bi truly value. Otherwise, if you are wary of my words and fear I’ll leak secrets, wouldn’t it just lead to the need to eliminate each other when an opportunity arises, seeking a clean resolution? I trust that as long as you stay in Cloudy Peak City for a while and show your face a few times, or take a trip to North Pavilion Country or Water Cloud Country to enjoy the scenery, the Water Dragon Sect will certainly come knocking. This is much better than you and Bai Bi meeting behind closed doors to conspire."

Huan Yun was taken aback for a moment before smiling, "That sounds best."

The next morning, at dawn, Sun Qing from the Colorful Sparrow House, along with her disciple Liu Guibao, arrived at Cloudy Peak City.

Shen Zhenze nearly jumped in anger but had no choice. When the two talisman boats had entered the city earlier, the enormous well had momentarily revealed its true form due to the mountain and water restrictions and protective formations.

It was likely that there were secret informants from the Colorful Sparrow House at the market, who immediately sent word to Peach Blossom Ferry.

This was quite normal; Cloudy Peak City also had secret informants at Peach Blossom Ferry.

Shen Zhenze wasn’t small-minded enough to outright deny Sun Qing entry into the city.

However, he still had the audacity to approach the residence.

If Sun Qing offered a higher price, Shen Zhenze couldn’t afford the well; would he raise the price to the point of absurdity? He wouldn’t make Shen Zhenze part with a single piece of celestial money.

In the end, if Sun Qing decided not to buy out of anger, Shen Zhenze could always sell off his possessions or even directly carve out a large piece of Cloudy Peak City land. If that still wasn’t enough, he could negotiate a loan or shamelessly borrow some money from Huan Yun.

In the yard, Chen Ping'an watched the sullen-faced Sun Qing and the leisurely raising prices Shen Zhenze.

As for the value of the well, Huan Yun couldn’t determine it either, merely stating that a price of eighty grain rain coins was certainly fair.

Chen Ping'an wore a serious expression, looking somewhat innocent and helpless.

In fact, he nearly gave Shen Zhenze a thumbs up.

Shen Zhenze had already bid up to eighty-six grain rain coins.

At this rate, Shen Zhenze could yell his price from morning till night, potentially raising it to a thousand.

Sun Qing said coldly, "Shen Zhenze, can we call it quits soon?"

Shen Zhenze smiled, "Is the Patriarch of the Sun House planning to part with it after much consideration? Then I should thank you, Patriarch Sun, on behalf of Cloudy Peak City."

Liu Guibao had remained silent the entire time.

In the yard, there were two young men and women accompanying Shen Zhenze. 

They were familiar faces—Xu Xingjiu and Zhao Qingwan.

Liu Guibao didn’t show much curiosity toward the black-robed man without a sword today; there were many oddities among the high-level cultivators in the mountains. Besides, his looks weren’t particularly impressive without the old man's mask; she saw nothing noteworthy.

However, she was keenly observing Xu Xingjiu and Zhao Qingwan, trying to uncover hints about them.

Could it be that the old immortal Huan Yun, while watching coldly, intentionally turned a blind eye to the actions of the former priest of Cloudy Peak City, actually had everything mapped out? Rather than employing a scheme to protect his reputation and obtain treasures, achieving two objectives in one go? If this were true, it would indeed be impressive.

Deep down, Chen Ping'an still hoped to sell the well to the Colorful Sparrow House.

Although Sun Daoren had left this grand world, Chen Ping'an could clearly see from Sun Daoren’s words and actions that he was rather fond of Liu Guibao. Though he ultimately decided against taking her as a disciple, citing “incompatibility with the Dao,” he still gifted her a book on the Dao. 

For Chen Ping'an, since he couldn’t carry this massive "grinding stone" around with him, it was better to go with the flow and sell it to the Colorful Sparrow House. After all, Sun Daoren had given him so many opportunities; Chen Ping'an felt he ought to do something in return to find peace of mind.

Even if it meant that they might never meet again in this lifetime.

Unless one day Chen Ping'an truly became an ascended great swordsman, then he might have the chance to venture into that realm of azure.

Some things can be done or not; if doing them would bring peace of mind, then there’s no need to hesitate.

Besides, it wouldn’t hinder his ability to earn money.

Suddenly, Sun Qing spoke to Chen Ping'an through thought, "Young Master Chen, how about thirty grain rain coins, and I’ll give you a treasure in return? Just give me a clear answer! If you don’t agree, I’ll leave right away! Rest assured, Young Master Chen, you are a valued guest of our Colorful Sparrow House. I never beat around the bush!"

That treasure was undoubtedly precious, but for Sun Qing, the well that could stabilize the fortunes of the mountains and waters was the true treasure.

Chen Ping'an was clearly taken aback.

After hesitating for a moment, he said, "Then it’s thirty grain rain coins, you can keep the treasure, and the remaining grain rain coins can be owed for now. Just tell me how much that treasure is worth in the mountains, and the Patriarch will repay me that many grain rain coins later."

Sun Qing actually refused, "The treasure is nothing but a trinket to me at the moment, even for the next hundred or so years. However, every grain rain coin earned by the Colorful Sparrow House is needed by Wu Qian and Liu Guibao— so many cultivators depend on these celestial coins. I can’t delay their training. Therefore, Young Master Chen, just say whether you are selling or not! Moreover, that treasure was something I inexplicably obtained, and I hadn’t even closed the door when I received Huan Lao's secret message, so I removed the restrictions. Young Master Chen can use it right away."

Finally, Sun Qing boldly declared, "If the deal falls through, we’ll still maintain our righteousness as valued guests; when Young Master Chen visits our Colorful Sparrow House next time, it’s uncertain whether you’ll have ordinary tea or that small mysterious wall!"

Chen Ping'an held back a laugh and replied through thought, "Then it's settled: thirty grain rain coins and a treasure."

Sun Qing burst into laughter, "Deal!"

There was no hiding her excitement at having made a deal with Young Master Chen.

Shen Zhenze felt a twinge of regret but was also fine with it.

What a stroke of luck to gain, and a fortune lost to fate.

Sun Qing turned to Shen Zhenze and said, "Regardless, the treasure was purchased by me in Cloudy Peak City, so consider it a favor I owe you."

Shen Zhenze nodded with a smile.

He took Xu Xingjiu and Zhao Qingwan along as they flew away on the wind.

Huan Yun gifted the Colorful Sparrow House a talisman boat.

Sun Qing graciously accepted it. 

Otherwise, would she really carry that well around while flying? What kind of shameless cultivator would do that?

Then, Sun Qing glanced at the well before shifting her gaze to the young swordsman named Chen.

Sun Qing soon felt relieved, thinking that it was likely due to her connection with the treasure that he had.

Chen Ping'an, aware of her thoughts, offered a calm smile.

Sun Qing felt a bit guilty. 

Her mother would undoubtedly owe the other party a great favor. Since he already possessed a treasure, this meant that the trinket she was about to part with wasn’t as valuable, leaving Sun Qing feeling somewhat helpless. It was fine though; after all, he was a friend of Liu Jinglong, and she had no reason to be overly polite with him.

Huan Yun, being perceptive, took his leave.

Sun Qing handed over the token treasure and thirty grain rain coins.

She then departed Cloudy Peak City with Liu Guibao and the well, aboard the talisman boat.

The head of the Colorful Sparrow House was grinning from ear to ear as she began drinking upon boarding the boat. She didn’t forget to look down and call out to Huan Yun, "Huan Zhenren, Cloudy Peak City isn’t very interesting; it’s just a palm-sized place where a fart in the east can be heard in the west. So, when you have time, do come visit our Colorful Sparrow House as a guest and serve as a priest; that would be even better!"

Shen Zhenze laughed and scolded, "Stop your nonsense! Huan Zhenren is already a nominal priest of Cloudy Peak City!"

Huan Yun shook his head with a smile.

But his mood was still quite pleasant.

Standing in the yard, with an extra treasure in hand, Chen Ping'an felt as if a pressing need had been resolved. He began organizing all his new and old items, categorizing them anew.

After a stick of incense had burned down, Huan Yun departed and returned.

Chen Ping'an was already seated in the pavilion atop the rockery, tilting his head and listening to the sound of the two grain rain coins clinking against each other.

Huan Yun sat opposite him, smiling as he remarked, "The room may be small, but the universe feels vast. A heart's thought can encompass the world; I used to think I understood it well, but now I realize I don’t."

Chen Ping'an continued to clink the coins, mumbling, "Knowing that you don’t know is a kind of knowing."

In truth, discussing profound principles with a Daoist Golden Core Earth Immortal made Chen Ping'an feel somewhat sheepish, but it was alright; many of his words were borrowed from his student Cui Dongshan.

Huan Yun chuckled, "If you can trust me, then I’ll set off to explore the mountains and rivers of North Pavilion Country."

Chen Ping'an put away the two grain rain coins, straightened up, and said, "I wish you success in overcoming your heart’s obstacles."

Huan Yun replied, "It’s still early. The time when I can clearly speak about this with Shen Zhenze and sincerely apologize to those two juniors will be when I have truly let go of my burdens."

Chen Ping'an nodded with a smile, "You haven’t lost your charm, old sir."

Huan Yun stood up and performed a respectful bow, "Take care, friend."

Chen Ping'an stood and clasped his fists in return, "Take care."

Huan Yun departed on the wind.

On the table was left a piece of talisman paper.

Chen Ping'an collected it, treating it as a temporary safeguard.

He didn’t even plan to open it.

Next, Chen Ping'an began to carefully consider what other heavenly materials and earthly treasures were needed to refine his wooden-based life-bound item. 

In fact, before setting off from the Ruined Mountain to North Julu Island, Cui Dongshan had provided a list. The materials varied for metal, wood, and fire, and he clearly stated that these were just the foundational materials for refining different life-bound items; having them ensured that one wouldn’t go wrong, but they were still far from enough. After all, every life-bound item in the world of five elements had its own nuances. It required the gentleman to seize opportunities and carefully explore them to succeed in the refinement process.

Chen Ping'an wasn’t in a hurry to leave Cloudy Peak City.

After all, the ferry to the Dragon Palace Cave would stop at Cloudy Peak City.

Every day, aside from cultivating, Chen Ping'an would still serve as a talisman vendor at the market.

On this day, he spotted a familiar face—Jin Shan.

The wild cultivator nearly knelt to the ground in greeting upon seeing Chen Ping'an, but was stopped in his tracks. Eventually, the two squatted together at the stall.

The man intended to return the unused attack talismans, along with the last remaining talisman with some spiritual energy left in it, to the elder.

Chen Ping'an shook his head, saying, "You should keep them; they aren’t worth much."

The man adamantly refused, his voice choked with emotion. 

What had begun as a seemingly harmless treasure-seeking trip had turned out to be so perilous—how many had survived in the end?

The man felt that one needed to uphold a sense of conscience.

So he had to make this trip to Cloudy Peak City, hoping to see the one who had lost "two of his mothers."

Chen Ping'an accepted the talismans.

He smiled and said, "Once we close up shop, how about we go for a drink?"

The man grinned, "Senior, let me take care of the tab, alright?"

Chen Ping'an nodded, "That works, but don’t expect any good wine."

The man’s grin widened; that made sense.

In the end, the man treated Chen Ping'an to a meal, though he felt a bit embarrassed for putting on a show. Yet he didn’t mind spending this money at all.

Cloudy Peak City had its own celestial ferry going back and forth.

The man spent a grain rain coin, boarded the ferry, and bid his farewell to the elder with a clasped fist. The elder remained courteous and polite, returning the gesture.

The ferry slowly drifted away.

After the meal, on the way to the ferry, the elder had returned the remaining talismans to him. He had to carefully hide them in his sleeve.

The elder also warned him to return home quickly, as the area around Cloudy Peak City was still not safe.

The man dared not take that lightly.

Earlier, they had talked about many things while drinking, from how his wife was virtuous and good at managing the household, to how their two children, though still young, had bright futures ahead of them. It wouldn’t be difficult for them to become scholars or even higher officials...

Now, with the alcohol wearing off, the man felt increasingly ashamed, slapping himself on the face.

After disembarking, he found a quiet spot to hide the talismans inside his boots, as he didn’t feel secure leaving them in his sleeves.

To his surprise, when he pulled them out, he discovered two golden talismans mixed in, which were completely different from the yellow paper ones he had previously.

The man stood there, dumbfounded.

He couldn’t help but recall something the elder had said during their drinking session.

"A swordsman acts for the sake of straightforwardness, not for reason."

*(End of Chapter)*

 ### Chapter 648: A Different Kind of Training (Part 1)

Chen Ping'an staggered back to his residence in Cloud City, reeking of alcohol. The walls of his home were inscribed with a circle of snow-mud talismans, effective against petty thieves, though they could do little against enlightened beings. Still, it was better than nothing.

Once inside the courtyard, Chen Ping'an shook his blue robe lightly, dissipating the scent of alcohol. He stepped into the place where Xu Gongfu practiced his Taoism year-round and settled onto a meditation mat that could draw in the spiritual energy of heaven and earth. The couplet he had hung on the back wall transformed the originally bare room into something akin to a study. He planned to hang it in the first floor of the bamboo house when he returned to Ruin Mountain, vowing never to sell it, treating it like a family heirloom, akin to the cursive calligraphy written by the county magistrate while intoxicated.

He took out a crimson Daoist jujube wood token, feeling the need to refine it immediately; otherwise, any Qi practitioner could easily enter once they acquired it, and merely refining the token's emptiness and gathering spiritual energy would be of little significance. 

In the world of refining, refining emptiness was like having a money talisman in hand—there would inevitably be gains and losses. Medium refinement, however, was akin to crafting an ancestral hall on a mountain peak, truly rooting in the Qi mansion, while large refinement involved the practitioner's life essence.

Before refining the nearby object, Chen Ping'an took out three treasures to admire, nourishing his spirit. Initially, within that water palace, he had conducted three transactions with the Daoist Sun. 

One was a lifelike wooden statue of the original Daoist Lord, exuding the beauty of wind and water. 

The second was a round fan, notable for its embroidery depicting a graceful lady holding the fan, playfully teasing a little yellow bird perched on a branch.

The third was a pair of Dragon King nets, inscribed with "Fighting Jiao" and "Hidden Coil."

Chen Ping'an intended to gift the wooden statue to Li Huai. As for the round fan, he decided it would be for the girl in the pink skirt. On Ruin Mountain, the busiest figure was not the steward Zhu Lian, nor the diligent Cen Yuanji, and certainly not the one who bathed in sunlight daily, Zheng Dafu, but rather the little girl Chen Ruchu. Chen Ping'an firmly believed that as long as Ruin Mountain existed, Chen Ruchu would remain tirelessly busy, carrying a water bucket and a cloth, with a jingling string of keys at her waist. Every day, without fail, she would greet Cui Cheng, pass some sunflower seeds to Pei Qian, water the flowers, and regularly visit the nearby town and county to procure necessary supplies. 

In Chen Ping'an's eyes, how could this not be considered a major affair? It was indeed significant.

Anyone with eyes could see it and should keep it in mind. 

Let alone the other practitioners outside Ruin Mountain in Longquan County, who would dare bully the girl in the pink skirt? Just try it! 

This wasn't favoritism on Chen Ping'an's part; rather, in his view, the girl in the pink skirt was the least likely to make mistakes, unmatched by anyone—himself included. 

Thus, he found it easy to converse with Daoist Sun. 

Listening to the wild cultivator Jin Shan talk about trivialities made Chen Ping'an feel quite pleased; it was a kind of comfort from two different sources.

He picked up a bamboo basket, and the other one gently shook in response. 

What he held in his hands were two genuine mountains of gold and silver.

As for how to arrange the Dragon King nets, Chen Ping'an felt somewhat uncertain. First, this pair had sustained significant damage and would require a large sum of divine money to repair. Second, although the Dragon King nets were immensely useful for catching dragons and similar beings, they were also quite particular; unlike many offensive treasures that could be used right away, if the nets lacked a unique divine technique, they might as well be throwing meat buns to dogs—vanishing without a trace.

After much contemplation, Chen Ping'an decided to take things one step at a time.

Since he now had an additional nearby object and didn't need to spend extra money, he definitely intended to purchase two swords forged at the Hate Sword Mountain, the sword cultivator's life essence. 

If the price were more affordable than anticipated, perhaps even three would suffice.

Upon reaching the Dragon Palace cave heaven, he'd first ascertain the price of the Dragon King nets and see if there were any big spenders willing to pay.

Such a rare item—why should he discuss repair costs with them? 

However, if he could avoid selling the Dragon King nets, he would. 

After all, every time it came to gifts, he couldn't keep using quantity to fool his first disciple; that just wasn't right.

Chen Ping'an began to calm his mind and gather his energy to refine the token. 

This task was not urgent, nor could it be completed in one go. 

Two hours later, he withdrew to a refining barrier and donned a robe, turning to refine the spiritual energy embodied within it. 

His mind settled. 

Unconsciously, the time reached the hour of the rat. Chen Ping'an opened his eyes, exhaled a heavy breath of turbid air, and waved his hand lightly to disperse it. 

According to Cui Dongshan's profound words, a small world of humanity had many lives exchanged. The practice of Qi practitioners emphasized refining the essence and discarding impurities, using heaven and earth's spiritual energy to temper bones, expand the Qi mansion, and cultivate the soul—all requiring meticulous effort.

Thus, practitioners were no longer mere mortals.

This was not merely a frightening saying. 

Chen Ping'an turned his consciousness to explore the Qi mansion. 

The water mansion remained unlocked, with a stream containing water spiritual energy flowing gently. This was merely the scene after Chen Ping'an had drained the dew drops from green bamboo leaves, without yet drawing the more refined and concentrated aqua energy from the azure bricks. The green-clad boys were increasingly busy, and the meticulously painted river murals in the water mansion were becoming more vibrant under their efforts.

The small pond suspended beneath the water character seal seemed to have expanded slightly, with the water deepening.

Chen Ping'an hesitated over whether to refine the aqua energy azure bricks from the Daoist temple and lay them down in the water mansion. 

Even without the faintest trace of aqua energy, the azure bricks were valuable in their own right.

He initially planned to take back the thirty-six aqua energy azure bricks to Ruin Mountain, which would perfectly pave six small paths for practicing the Six Steps of the Mountain Shaking Fist. 

There would be himself, Pei Qian, Zhu Lian, Zheng Dafu, Cen Yuanji. 

Of course, there was also the highly compatible Lu Baixiang.

As for Wei Xian, he could be left out. 

As for Sui You, he was already at the Yuguizong on Tongyezhou, transitioning from a pure martial artist to a practitioner, hoping to become a female sword immortal who could soar with her sword in the realm of righteousness.

However, if the azure bricks could enhance the water mansion, then the six bricks belonging to Chen Ping'an could definitely be refined.

With the water character seal above, azure bricks on the floor, and murals on the walls, Chen Ping'an felt that this way, his water mansion could be considered quite impressive.

As for the one hundred and twenty-two green glazed tiles, he would keep them for now, as their origins were unclear. 

Huan Yun had also not dared to rashly conclude anything, only confirming that they were undoubtedly worth a fortune. If they were of the same origin as the Glazed Pavilion in the White Emperor City of the Central Plains, that would be even more astonishing.

Legend had it that the most precious items in the Glazed Pavilion, besides the twelve glazed beams, were the glazed tiles atop the roof.

Chen Ping'an retracted his spirit, rose from the room, and began practicing the Six Steps of the Mountain Shaking Fist in the courtyard. 

Unexpectedly, a visitor hurriedly arrived.

It was Wu Qian, the Grandmaster of the Colorful Sparrow Manor, his face bursting with joy.

Chen Ping'an led Wu Qian to the pavilion atop the artificial hill. Wu Qian had come to present Chen Ping'an with a first-rate robe from the Colorful Sparrow Manor. 

Wu Qian mentioned that a certain well had been moved to the manor and was remarkably compatible with their landscape. Not only could it stabilize the terrain, but it could also gather luck from all directions. Even without refining it yet, merely placing it in the ancestral hall had already shown miraculous signs. After refining it, it would be a foundation item that only sects and ancestral halls could possess. Thus, the deal with Cloud City had been far too profitable for her, and feeling guilty, she had to send a robe as compensation. If Chen Jianxian refused, that was fine; she had already been polite, and if Chen Jianxian also followed suit, then she wouldn't hold back.

Chen Ping'an repeatedly said he wouldn't be polite, accepting the exquisitely crafted robe from Wu Qian and placing it into his token.

The only downside was that the robe's style was too flamboyant—less to his taste than the snowflake robe worn by the ghostly woman of Skin City, which he could wear comfortably.

Wu Qian didn't linger long, but left behind several large jars of tea, saying this was the remaining small Xuanbi from the Colorful Sparrow Manor this year. 

Wu Qian added with a smile, "If Chen Jianxian plans to sell it, please do sell it for a high price; otherwise, it wouldn't do justice to the name of the small Xuanbi."

Chen Ping'an felt a bit embarrassed and said, "Please inform Manor Master Sun that I will set aside a jar of small Xuanbi as a gift."

Wu Qian smiled knowingly and nodded, taking off on the wind.

Just as Wu Qian left, Shen Zhenze arrived. 

Chen Ping'an had just sat down and had to rise to greet him.

The lord of Cloud City chuckled, "Wu Qian wouldn't be inviting you, Chen Xiansheng, to be a mountain offering, would she? You mustn't go, you mustn't go! It's just a lot of fluttering flowers that will distract you from your practice."

Chen Ping'an shook his head, "The Colorful Sparrow Manor has no such intentions."
